**元智大學管理學院財務金融暨會計碩士班**

**（Master of Science in Finance and Accounting）**

**必修科目表**

**（104學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required and Elective Courses**

**(For students, entrance in academic year 104)**

104.04.22 一○三學年度第五次教務會議通過

104.07.01 一○三學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

105.01.20 一○四學年度第三次教務會議修訂通過

105.04.20 一○四學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

105.06.22 一○四學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>學期</p><p>科目</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506</p><p>( 3 )</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分</p><p>小計</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）及「會計」（MS in Accounting）兩個主修領域。</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求為最低總畢業學分數39學分，另加碩士論文一篇。</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目15學分及選修科目至少21學分，主修會計領域必修科目21學分及選修科目至少15學分，與各項規定要求。</li><li>主修財務金融學程：碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上（電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上），或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。</li><li>主修會計學程：碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗600分以上（電腦測驗250分、新托福測驗IBT100以上）或IELTS 6.5以上或多益(TOEIC)890分以上，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。</li><li>財務金融暨會計碩士班學生修習「海外研習」與「企業專案實習」（實習期間由本院企業實習辦法規範），各學程採認／抵免說明如下：主修財務金融學程：選修「企業專案實習」不列入選修學分，僅可抵免「財務金融專題研討（三）」或「財務金融專題研討（四）」，以一次為限；主修會計學程：「海外研習」與「企業專案實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。</li><li>碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

<table><tr><td><p>Subjects</p></td><td><p>Course No</p></td><td><p>Course Title in Chinese</p></td><td><p>Course Title in English</p></td><td><p>Credits</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="3"><p>Elective Courses of Finance </p></td><td><p>CM520</p></td><td><p>數量方法</p></td><td><p>Quantitative Methods</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>CM631</p></td><td><p>金融市場與機構</p></td><td><p>Financial Market and Institution </p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>CM526</p></td><td><p>衍生性金融商品</p></td><td><p>Derivative Securities</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>Elective Courses of Accounting</p></td><td><p>CM531</p></td><td><p>財務會計與資本市場</p></td><td><p>Financial Accounting and Capital Markets</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>CM533</p></td><td><p>會計研究方法</p></td><td><p>Empirical Accounting</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本碩士班畢業要求為最低總畢業學分數39學分，另加碩士論文一篇。申請上學期口試者須於12月底前完成論文口試，申請下學期口試者須於6月底前完成論文口試。</li></ol><p>Graduation requirements: Students must take a minimum of 39 credits and complete a master thesis. Oral defense of thesis must be completed by the end of December for Fall graduation and by the end of June for Spring graduation.</p><ol><li>具備中文能力之外籍生得適用本籍生適用之所屬主修領域修業規定。</li></ol><p>Foreign students with Chinese ability are eligible to choose the course requirements for domestic students of their major program.</p><ol><li>碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。</li></ol><p>Students must take “English for Business Professionals” or “International Business Communication” arranged by the College (not lead to graduation credits). These courses can be waived if students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level. For students from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand or received bachelor degrees from listed countries, these courses can be waived.</p><ol><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Students must choose an advisor of their programs.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。</li></ol><p>Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first academic year and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</p><p>6.碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。</p><p>Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</p><p>7.研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。</p><p>Students have to pass their proposal of graduated thesis application before the second weeks of the second academic year. The oral committee have to include the advisor (and the joint advisor if you have) and the other committee member, the qualification of committee member doesn’t restrict in teaching in YZU. If students could not pass the first oral, they have to apply a new proposal in one month, and he/ she could not apply the final graduated thesis oral examination in six months.8. </p><p>8.外籍生除所屬主修領域必選修課程外，不足之學分可跨領域選修管院其他碩士學程之外籍生必選修課程。海外研習課程不認列畢業學分數。</p><p>Foreign students should take required and elective courses of their major program as priority; students can choose elective courses in other master programs.</p><p>Program will not recognize of overseas study into account.</p><p>9.主修財金學程之外籍生須修習財務金融專題研討(一)～(四)，並參加英文演講之場次。非財務金融專題研討(一)～(四)之其他專題研討課程，至多承認6學分為畢業學分。</p><p>Foreign students major in Finance are required to take the courses of finance seminar (1)~(4), and participate in the English speeches. Non-finance seminar courses will be record no more than six credits.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

# 元智大學管理學院財務金融暨會計碩士班（Master of Science in Finance and Accounting）必修科目表

（106學年度入學新生適用） List of Required and Elective Courses (For students, entrance in academic year 106)

107.05.02 一○六學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017, on May 2, 2018 107.11.21 一○七學年度第三次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 3rd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2018, on November 21, 2018

<table><tr><td rowspan="2">學年 學期 科目</td><td>第一學年</td><td colspan="2">第二學年</td></tr><tr><td>上 下</td><td>上</td><td>下</td></tr><tr><td>MS 必 修 科 目 (3)</td><td>計量經濟學 (Econometrics) CM506 （3）</td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td>學期學分 小計</td><td>3 0 1.本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）及「會計」（MS in</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>備 註</td><td colspan="4">Accounting）兩個主修領域。 2.本碩士班畢業要求為最低總畢業學分數39學分，另加碩士論文一篇。 3.碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目18學分及選修科目至少18學分， 主修會計領域必修科目 24學分及選修科目至少12學分，與各項規定要求。主修財務金融領域者， 至少須修習18學分以上之英語授課課程。 4.主修財務金融學程：碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分)。 惟，若該生 TOEFL/ITP 考試紙筆測驗 520分以上(電腦測驗 190分新托福測驗 IBT68以上)，或 IELTS6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675 分以上，或全民英 檢中高級，得提出申請日前五年內之有效證明，申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美 國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申 請免修。 5.主修會計學程：碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分)。惟， 若該生 TOEFL/ITP 考試紙筆測驗 600 分以上(電腦測驗 250分新托福測驗 IBT100 以上)或 IELTS 6.5 以上或多益(TOEIC)890 分以上，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國加拿 大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。 6.財務金融暨會計碩士班學生修習「海外研習」與「企業專案實習」（實習期間由本院企業實習辦法規 範)，各學程採認/抵免說明如下：主修財務金融學程：選修「企業專案實習」不列入選修學分，僅可 抵免「財務金融專題研討（三)」或「財務金融專題研討（四)」，以一次為限；主修會計學程：「海外 研習」與「企業專案實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。 7.碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。 8.碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。 9.碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。 10. 碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。 11．  研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教 授)及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不 得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。 12．入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研 究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。 13．若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。</td></tr></table>

Oral defense of thesis must be completed by the end of December for Fall graduation and by the end of June for Spring graduation.</li><li>具備中文能力之外籍生得適用本籍生適用之所屬主修領域修業規定。Foreign students with Chinese ability are eligible to choose the course requirements for domestic students of their major program.</li><li>碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。Students must take “English for Business Professionals” or “International Business Communication” arranged by the College (not lead to graduation credits). These courses can be waived if students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level. For students from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand or received bachelor degrees from listed countries, these courses can be waived.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Students must choose an advisor of their programs.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first academic year and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。Students have to pass their proposal of graduated thesis application before the second weeks of the second academic year. The oral committee have to include the advisor (and the joint advisor if you have) and the other committee member, the qualification of committee member doesn’t restrict in teaching in YZU. If students could not pass the first oral, they have to apply a new proposal in one month, and he/ she could not apply the final graduated thesis oral examination in six months.8. </li><li>外籍生除所屬主修領域必選修課程外，不足之學分可跨領域選修管院其他碩士/博士學程之外籍生必選修課程。Foreign students should take required and elective courses of their major program as priority; students can choose elective courses in other master /PhD programs.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506 (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分</p><p>小計</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）、「會計」（MS in Accounting）及「金融科技」（MS in Financial Technology）三個主修領域。</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求各學程主修財務金融領域與會計領域最低總畢業學分數36學分，主修金融科技領域最低總畢業學分數24學分，以上三個主修領域皆須加碩士論文一篇。</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目18學分、必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少6學分，主修會計領域必修科目15學分及選修科目至少18學分，主修金融科技領域必修科目21學分，與各項規定要求。主修金融科技領域碩士生得以「金融大數據分析與預測」作為MS必修科目3學分，另外再加修金融科技領域選修科目至少3學分。</li><li>主修財務金融學程：碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6.0以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得提出申請日前五年內之有效證明，申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。</li><li>主修會計學程：碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗600分以上(電腦測驗250分、新托福測驗IBT100以上)或IELTS 6.5以上或多益(TOEIC)890分以上，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。</li><li>主修金融科技學程：(1) 碩士生需修習過投資學或具備2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗，並提出修課證明或工作證明。若無修過投資學，亦無2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗者，需修習大學部「投資學」，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(2) 碩士生需在學校單位或公私立培訓機構修習過程式設計課、程式培訓課程、或程式設計工作坊，並提出修課證明。若無修習過程式設計者，需修習大學部「Python程式設計」課程或類似課名課程，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。</li><li>主修會計學程：「海外研習」與「企業專案實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。</li><li>碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。</li></ol></td></tr></table>

Oral defense of thesis must be completed by the end of December for Fall graduation and by the end of June for Spring graduation.</li><li>具備中文能力之外籍生得適用本籍生適用之所屬主修領域修業規定。Foreign students with Chinese ability are eligible to choose the course requirements for domestic students of their major program.</li><li>碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者，亦得提出證明，申請免修。Students must take “English for Business Professionals” or “International Business Communication” arranged by the College (not lead to graduation credits). These courses can be waived if students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level. For students from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand or received bachelor degrees from listed countries, these courses can be waived.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Students must choose an advisor of their programs.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first academic year and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。Students have to pass their proposal of graduated thesis application before the second weeks of the second academic year. The oral committee have to include the advisor (and the joint advisor if you have) and the other committee member, the qualification of committee member doesn’t restrict in teaching in YZU. If students could not pass the first oral, they have to apply a new proposal in one month, and he/ she could not apply the final graduated thesis oral examination in six months.8. </li><li>外籍生除所屬主修領域必選修課程外，不足之學分可跨領域選修管院其他碩士/博士學程之外籍生必選修課程。Foreign students should take required and elective courses of their major program as priority; students can choose elective courses in other master/PhD programs<s>.</s></li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td><td><p>上</p></td><td><p>下</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506 (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分</p><p>小計</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）、「會計」（MS in Accounting）及「金融科技」（MS in Financial Technology）三個主修領域。</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求各學程主修財務金融領域與會計領域最低總畢業學分數36學分，主修金融科技領域最低總畢業學分數24學分，以上三個主修領域皆須加碩士論文一篇。</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目18學分、必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少6學分，主修會計領域必修科目15學分及選修科目至少18學分，主修金融科技領域必修科目21學分，與各項規定要求。主修金融科技領域碩士生得以「金融大數據分析與預測」作為MS必修科目3學分，另外再加修金融科技領域選修科目至少3學分。</li><li>各學程相關規定：</li><li>主修財務金融：(i) 碩士生需在畢業前達到以下任何一項英語標準：(a) TOEIC 675分，或TOEFL iBT 68分，或CEFR 語言能力參考指標B2等級之英語檢定；(b) 修習本學程英語授課學分數達15學分且成績達70分(含)以上；(c) 修習本院商用英文(CM740)課程或本院碩士班以上英語授課課程且成績達70分(含)以上，此課程不計入修業學分；(d) 國籍為美國、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭或英語為官方語言之國家，或曾於前述國家取得大學以上學位，經學程召集人同意。(ii)碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。</li><li>主修會計學程：(i)碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6.0以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得提出申請日前五年內之有效證明，申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者或官方語言為英語且經學程召集人同意，得申請免修。(ii)「海外研習」與「企業專案實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。(iii)碩士生經學程召集人同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。</li><li>主修金融科技學程：(i) 碩士生需修習過投資學或具備2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗，並提出修課證明或工作證明。若無修過投資學，亦無2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗者，需修習大學部「投資學」，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(ii) 碩士生需在學校單位或公私立培訓機構修習過程式設計課、程式培訓課程、或程式設計工作坊，並提出修課證明。若無修習過程式設計者，需修習大學部「Python程式設計」課程或類似課名課程，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(iii)碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。</li></ol></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p>Subjects</p></td><td><p>Course No</p></td><td><p>Course Title in Chinese</p></td><td><p>Course Title in English</p></td><td><p>Credits</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>Elective Courses of Accounting</p></td><td><p>CM534</p></td><td><p>財務報表分析</p></td><td><p>Financial Statement Analysis</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本碩士班畢業要求為最低總畢業學分數36學分，另加碩士論文一篇。申請上學期口試者須於12月底前完成論文口試，申請下學期口試者須於6月底前完成論文口試。Graduation requirements: Students must take a minimum of 36 credits and complete a master thesis. Oral defense of thesis must be completed by the end of December for Fall graduation and by the end of June for Spring graduation.</li><li>具備中文能力之外籍生得適用本籍生適用之所屬主修領域修業規定。Foreign students with Chinese ability are eligible to choose the course requirements for domestic students of their major program.</li><li>碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者或官方語言為英語且經學程召集人同意，得申請免修。Students must take “English for Business Professionals” or “International Business Communication” arranged by the College (this course can't be used as credits for Graduation). If students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level, or students are from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand, have received bachelor degrees from listed countries, or official language is English and gets approval from the director of the discipline , these courses can be waived.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Students must choose an advisor of their programs.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first academic year and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。Students have to pass their proposal of graduated thesis application before the second weeks of the second academic year. The oral committee have to include the advisor (and the joint advisor if you have) and the other committee member, the qualification of committee member doesn’t restrict in teaching in YZU. If students could not pass the first oral, they have to apply a new proposal in one month, and he/ she could not apply the final graduated thesis oral examination in six months.8. </li><li>外籍生除所屬主修領域必選修課程外，不足之學分可跨領域選修管院其他碩士/博士學程之外籍生必選修課程。Foreign students should take required and elective courses of their major program as priority; students can choose elective courses in other master/PhD programs<s>.</s></li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂
```

**元智大學管理學院財務金融暨會計碩士班**

**（Master of Science in Finance and Accounting）**

**必修科目表**

**（110學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required and Elective Courses**

**(For students, entrance in academic year 110)**

110.05.05 一○九學年度第五次教務會議通過

110.06.16 一○九學年度第六次教務會議通過

111.12.28 一一一學年度第三次教務會議通過

113.01.03 一一二學年度第六次教務會議通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Course Name</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年First Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年Second Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上First Term</p></td><td><p>下Second Term</p></td><td><p>上First Term</p></td><td><p>下Second Term</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>MS</p><p>Required Course</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506 (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Subtotal of Semester Credits </p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）、「會計」（MS in Accounting）及「金融科技」（MS in Financial Technology）三個主修領域。The Master’s Program in Financial and Accounting (MS Program) of this institution includes three major fields: "Finance" (MS in Finance), "Accounting" (MS in Accounting), and "Financial Technology" (MS in Financial Technology).</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求各學程主修財務金融領域與會計領域最低總畢業學分數36學分，主修金融科技領域最低總畢業學分數24學分，以上三個主修領域皆須加碩士論文一篇。The graduation requirements for this master’s program include a minimum of 36 credits for the Finance and Accounting major fields, and a minimum of 24 credits for the Financial Technology major field. All three major fields must also include the completion of a master’s thesis.</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目18學分、必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少6學分，主修會計領域必修科目15學分及選修科目至少18學分，主修金融科技領域必修科目21學分，與各項規定要求。主修金融科技領域碩士生得以「金融大數據分析與預測」作為MS必修科目3學分，另外再加修金融科技領域選修科目至少3學分。Graduate students must complete 3 credits of MS core courses. For the Finance major, students are required to complete 18 credits of compulsory courses, 9 credits of compulsory elective courses, and at least 6 credits of elective courses. For the Accounting major, students must complete 15 credits of compulsory courses and at least 18 credits of elective courses. For the Financial Technology major, students must complete 3 credits of compulsory courses, and "Financial Big Data Analysis and Forecasting" can be counted as part of the 3 credits of MS core courses. Students also need to complete 21 credits of compulsory elective courses.</li><li>各學程相關規定：Specific Requirements:</li><li>主修財務金融：(i) 碩士生需在畢業前達到以下任何一項英語標準：(a) TOEIC 675分，或TOEFL iBT 68分，或CEFR 語言能力參考指標B2等級之英語檢定；(b) 修習本學程英語授課學分數達15學分且成績達70分(含)以上；(c) 修習本院商用英文(CM740)課程或本院碩士班以上英語授課課程且成績達70分(含)以上，此課程不計入修業學分；(d) 國籍為美國、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭或英語為官方語言之國家，或曾於前述國家取得大學以上學位，經學程召集人同意。(ii)碩士生經學群會議同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。(1) MS in Finance: (i) Before graduation, master’s students must meet one of the following English language proficiency standards: (a) TOEIC score of 675, or TOEFL iBT score of 68, or CEFR B2 level English proficiency test score; (b) Complete 15 credits of English-taught courses in this program with a grade of 70 or above; (c) Complete the Business English course (CM740) or other English-taught courses at the master's level in this institution with a grade of 70 or above. This course does not count towards graduation credits; (d) Students whose nationality is from the United States, the United Kingdom, Australia, New Zealand, or any country where English is an official language, or who have previously studied in any of these countries. (ii) With the consent of the academic program meeting, students may take courses from other master’s programs in this institution. </li><li>主修會計學程：(i)碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6.0以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得提出申請日前五年內之有效證明，申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者或官方語言為英語且經學程召集人同意，得申請免修。</li></ol></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p><a></a>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td><p>(ii)「海外研習」與「企業專案實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。(iii)碩士生經學程召集人同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。(2) MS in Accounting: (i) Master's students are required to complete the "Business English" course offered by the college (not counted toward graduation credits). However, students may apply for an exemption if they can provide valid proof, issued within five years before the application date, meeting one of the following criteria: TOEFL/ITP paper-based test score of 520 or above (computer-based test: 190, TOEFL iBT: 68 or above)IELTS score of 6.0 or above. GMAT score in the top 70% or above. GRE score in the top 70% or above. TOEIC score of 675 or above. High-intermediate level of the General English Proficiency Test (GEPT). In addition, international students may apply for an exemption if they are from English-speaking countries (limited to the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, Australia, or New Zealand), have earned a university degree or higher from one of these countries, or if their official language is English and the exemption is approved by the program director. (ii) Students may choose to recognize Overseas Study or Corporate Internship as a course, but only one of the two, and only once. (iii) With the approval of the program coordinator, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master's programs offered by the institute.</p><ol><li>主修金融科技學程：(i) 碩士生需修習過投資學或具備2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗，並提出修課證明或工作證明。若無修過投資學，亦無2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗者，需修習大學部「投資學」，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(ii) 碩士生需在學校單位或公私立培訓機構修習過程式設計課、程式培訓課程、或程式設計工作坊，並提出修課證明。若無修習過程式設計者，需修習大學部「Python程式設計」課程或類似課名課程，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(iii)碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Financial Technology: (i) Students must have completed a course in Investments or possess at least two years of practical experience in finance-related work, providing proof of coursework or work experience. If neither requirement is met, students must take the undergraduate course Investments and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (ii) Students must have taken a programming course, training program, or workshop at the university or other training institutions and provide proof of completion. If no prior programming experience exists, students must take the undergraduate course Python Programming or a similar course and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (iii) With approval from their advisor or supervisor, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master’s programs offered by the institute.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Master's students must select their thesis advisor from professors in their major field of study.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Master's students are required to select their thesis advisor and complete the registration process by the end of the first academic year. They must also complete the thesis oral defense as stipulated.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。If a master's student fails two or more required courses by the end of the first academic year, they may extend the deadline for selecting a thesis advisor by six months.</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。By the second week of the second semester of the second year, graduate students must pass the oral defense of their thesis proposal. The oral defense committee must consist of the advisor (including co-advisors, if any) and one committee member, who may be from within or outside the university. If a student fails the first attempt, a re-submission is required within one month. Students who do not pass the thesis proposal oral defense are not allowed to apply for the final thesis oral defense within six months.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。Newly admitted graduate students must complete the academic research ethics education program as specified in the university's guidelines by the end of their first semester. The latest they can complete this program is before applying for the degree oral defense. Students who fail to complete the program cannot apply for the degree oral defense.</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。Matters not addressed herein shall be governed by the academic regulations of each major field of study.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

credits.</li><li>必修課與選修課以本班各學程所開課程為主。未列在選修科目但為管理學院各碩士班學程所開的課程，至多得認列選修科目3學分。The required and elective courses are based on the courses offered by each program within this class. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。Students have to pass their proposal of graduated thesis application before the second weeks of the second academic year. The oral committee have to include the advisor (and the joint advisor if you have) and the other committee member, the qualification of committee member doesn’t restrict in teaching in YZU. If students could not pass the first oral, they have to apply a new proposal in one month, and he/ she could not apply the final graduated thesis oral examination in six months.8. </li><li>外籍生除所屬主修領域必選修課程外，不足之學分可跨領域選修管院其他碩士/博士學程之外籍生必選修課程。Foreign students should take required and elective courses of their major program as priority; students can choose elective courses in other master/PhD programs<s>.</s></li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

**元智大學管理學院財務金融暨會計碩士班**

**（Master of Science in Finance and Accounting）**

**必修科目表**

**（111學年度入學新生適用）**

**(For students, entrance in academic year 111)**

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

113.01.03 一一二學年度第六次教務會議通過

<table><tr><td colspan="3" rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subjects</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 First Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年Second Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(3)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>Required</p><p>Courses</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506</p><p> (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3"><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Semester Credit Subtotal</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="5"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）、「會計」（MS in Accounting）及「金融科技」（MS in Financial Technology）三個主修領域。The Master’s Program in Financial and Accounting (MS Program) of this institution includes three major fields: "Finance" (MS in Finance), "Accounting" (MS in Accounting), and "Financial Technology" (MS in Financial Technology).</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求各學程主修財務金融領域與會計領域最低總畢業學分數36學分，主修金融科技領域最低總畢業學分數24學分，以上三個主修領域皆須加碩士論文一篇。The graduation requirements for this master’s program include a minimum of 36 credits for the Finance and Accounting major fields, and a minimum of 24 credits for the Financial Technology major field. All three major fields must also include the completion of a master’s thesis.</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目18學分、必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少6學分，主修會計領域必修科目15學分及選修科目至少18學分，主修金融科技領域必修科目21學分，與各項規定要求。主修金融科技領域碩士生得以「金融大數據分析與預測」作為MS必修科目3學分，另外再加修金融科技領域選修科目至少3學分。Graduate students must complete 3 credits of MS core courses. For the Finance major, students are required to complete 18 credits of compulsory courses, 9 credits of compulsory elective courses, and at least 6 credits of elective courses. For the Accounting major, students must complete 15 credits of compulsory courses and at least 18 credits of elective courses. For the Financial Technology major, students must complete 3 credits of compulsory courses, and "Financial Big Data Analysis and Forecasting" can be counted as part of the 3 credits of MS core courses. Students also need to complete 21 credits of compulsory elective courses.</li><li>各學程相關規定：Specific Requirements:</li><li>主修財務金融：(i) 碩士生需在畢業前達到以下任何一項英語標準：(a) TOEIC 675分，或TOEFL iBT 68分，或CEFR 語言能力參考指標B2等級之英語檢定；(b) 修習本學程英語授課學分數達15學分且成績達70分(含)以上；(c) 修習本院商用英文(CM740)課程或本院碩士班以上英語授課課程且成績達70分(含)以上，此課程不計入修業學分；(d) 國籍為美國、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭或英語為官方語言之國家，或曾於前述國家取得大學以上學位，經學程召集人同意。(ii)碩士生經學群會議同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。(1) MS in Finance: (i) Before graduation, master’s students must meet one of the following English language proficiency standards: (a) TOEIC score of 675, or TOEFL iBT score of 68, or CEFR B2 level English proficiency test score; (b) Complete 15 credits of English-taught courses in this program with a grade of 70 or above; (c) Complete the Business English course (CM740) or other English-taught courses at the master's level in this institution with a grade of 70 or above. This course does not count towards graduation credits; (d) Students whose nationality is from the United States, the United Kingdom, Australia, New Zealand, or any country where English is an official language, or who have previously studied in any of these countries. (ii) With the consent of the academic program meeting, students may take courses from other master’s programs in this institution.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p><a></a>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>主修會計學程：(i)「海外研習」與「企業實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。(ii) 碩士生經學程召集人同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Accounting: (i) Students may choose to recognize Overseas Study or Corporate Internship as a course, but only one of the two, and only once. (ii) With the approval of the program coordinator, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master's programs offered by the institute.</li><li>主修金融科技學程：(i) 碩士生需修習過投資學或具備2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗，並提出修課證明或工作證明。若無修過投資學，亦無2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗者，需修習大學部「投資學」，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(ii) 碩士生需在學校單位或公私立培訓機構修習過程式設計課、程式培訓課程、或程式設計工作坊，並提出修課證明。若無修習過程式設計者，需修習大學部「Python程式設計」課程或類似課名課程，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(iii)碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Financial Technology: (i) Students must have completed a course in Investments or possess at least two years of practical experience in finance-related work, providing proof of coursework or work experience. If neither requirement is met, students must take the undergraduate course Investments and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (ii) Students must have taken a programming course, training program, or workshop at the university or other training institutions and provide proof of completion. If no prior programming experience exists, students must take the undergraduate course Python Programming or a similar course and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (iii) With approval from their advisor or supervisor, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master’s programs offered by the institute.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Master's students must select their thesis advisor from professors in their major field of study.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Master's students are required to select their thesis advisor and complete the registration process by the end of the first academic year. They must also complete the thesis oral defense as stipulated.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。If a master's student fails two or more required courses by the end of the first academic year, they may extend the deadline for selecting a thesis advisor by six months.</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。By the second week of the second semester of the second year, graduate students must pass the oral defense of their thesis proposal. The oral defense committee must consist of the advisor (including co-advisors, if any) and one committee member, who may be from within or outside the university. If a student fails the first attempt, a re-submission is required within one month. Students who do not pass the thesis proposal oral defense are not allowed to apply for the final thesis oral defense within six months.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。Newly admitted graduate students must complete the academic research ethics education program as specified in the university's guidelines by the end of their first semester. The latest they can complete this program is before applying for the degree oral defense. Students who fail to complete the program cannot apply for the degree oral defense.</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。Matters not addressed herein shall be governed by the academic regulations of each major field of study.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

If students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level, or students are from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand, have received bachelor degrees from listed countries, or official language is English and gets approval from the director of the discipline , these courses can be waived.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Students must choose an advisor of their programs.</li><li>碩士生應於入學後第二學期開學後一個月內選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first month in the second semester and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研二下學期開學第二個星期內需通過論文計畫書口試，口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。若第一次未通過者，必須於一個月內補提；未通過論文計畫書口試者不得於六個月內提畢業論文口試。Students have to pass their proposal of graduated thesis application before the second weeks of the second academic year. The oral committee have to include the advisor (and the joint advisor if you have) and the other committee member, the qualification of committee member doesn’t restrict in teaching in YZU. If students could not pass the first oral, they have to apply a new proposal in one month, and he/ she could not apply the final graduated thesis oral examination in six months.8. </li><li>外籍生除所屬主修領域必選修課程外，不足之學分可跨領域選修管院其他碩士/博士學程之外籍生必選修課程。Foreign students should take required and elective courses of their major program as priority; students can choose elective courses in other master/PhD programs<s>.</s></li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

**元智大學管理學院財務金融暨會計碩士班**

**（Master of Science in Finance and Accounting）**

**必修科目表**

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required and Elective Courses**

**(For students, entrance in academic year 112)**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

112.11.22 一一二學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

113.01.03 一一二學年度第六次教務會議通過

113.06.05 一一二學年度第九次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subjects</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 First Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年Second Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>Required</p><p>Courses</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506 (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Semester Credit Subtotal</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="5"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）、「會計」（MS in Accounting）及「金融科技」（MS in Financial Technology）三個主修領域。The Master’s Program in Financial and Accounting (MS Program) of this institution includes three major fields: "Finance" (MS in Finance), "Accounting" (MS in Accounting), and "Financial Technology" (MS in Financial Technology).</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求各學程主修財務金融領域與會計領域最低總畢業學分數36學分，主修金融科技領域最低總畢業學分數24學分，以上三個主修領域皆須加碩士論文一篇。The graduation requirements for this master’s program include a minimum of 36 credits for the Finance and Accounting major fields, and a minimum of 24 credits for the Financial Technology major field. All three major fields must also include the completion of a master’s thesis.</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目18學分、必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少6學分，主修會計領域必修科目12學分，必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少12學分，主修金融科技領域必修科目3學分，得以「金融大數據分析與預測」作為MS必修科目3學分，必選修科目12學分及選修科目至少6學分。Graduate students must complete 3 credits of MS core courses. For the Finance major, students are required to complete 18 credits of compulsory courses, 9 credits of compulsory elective courses, and at least 6 credits of elective courses. For the Accounting major, students must complete 12 credits of compulsory courses, 9 credits of compulsory elective courses, and at least 12 credits of elective courses. For the Financial Technology major, students must complete 3 credits of compulsory courses, and "Financial Big Data Analysis and Forecasting" can be counted as part of the 3 credits of MS core courses. Students also need to complete 12 credits of compulsory elective courses and at least 6 credits of elective courses.</li><li>各學程相關規定：Specific Requirements:</li><li>主修財務金融：(i) 碩士生需在畢業前達到以下任何一項英語標準：(a) TOEIC 675分，或TOEFL iBT 68分，或CEFR 語言能力參考指標B2等級之英語檢定；(b) 修習本學程英語授課學分數達15學分且成績達70分(含)以上；(c) 修習本院商用英文(CM740)課程或本院碩士班以上英語授課課程且成績達70分(含)以上，此課程不計入修業學分；(d) 國籍為美國、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭或英語為官方語言之國家，或曾於前述國家取(ii)碩士生經學群會議同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。(1) MS in Finance: (i) Before graduation, master’s students must meet one of the following English language proficiency standards: (a) TOEIC score of 675, or TOEFL iBT score of 68, or CEFR B2 level English proficiency test score; (b) Complete 15 credits of English-taught courses in this program with a grade of 70 or above; (c) Complete the Business English course (CM740) or other English-taught courses at the master's level in this institution with a grade of 70 or above. This course does not count towards graduation credits; (d) Students whose nationality is from the United States, the United Kingdom, Australia, New Zealand, or any country where English is an official language, or who have previously studied in any of these countries. (ii) With the consent of the academic program meeting, students may take courses from other master’s programs in this institution.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p><a></a>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>主修會計學程：(i)「海外研習」與「企業實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。(ii) 碩士生經學程召集人同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Accounting: (i) Students may choose to recognize Overseas Study or Corporate Internship as a course, but only one of the two, and only once. (ii) With the approval of the program coordinator, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master's programs offered by the institute.</li><li>主修金融科技學程：(i) 碩士生需修習過投資學或具備2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗，並提出修課證明或工作證明。若無修過投資學，亦無2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗者，需修習大學部「投資學」，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(ii) 碩士生需在學校單位或公私立培訓機構修習過程式設計課、程式培訓課程、或程式設計工作坊，並提出修課證明。若無修習過程式設計者，需修習大學部「Python程式設計」課程或類似課名課程，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(iii)碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Financial Technology: (i) Students must have completed a course in Investments or possess at least two years of practical experience in finance-related work, providing proof of coursework or work experience. If neither requirement is met, students must take the undergraduate course Investments and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (ii) Students must have taken a programming course, training program, or workshop at the university or other training institutions and provide proof of completion. If no prior programming experience exists, students must take the undergraduate course Python Programming or a similar course and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (iii) With approval from their advisor or supervisor, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master’s programs offered by the institute.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Master's students must select their thesis advisor from professors in their major field of study.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Master's students are required to select their thesis advisor and complete the registration process by the end of the first academic year. They must also complete the thesis oral defense as stipulated.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。If a master's student fails two or more required courses by the end of the first academic year, they may extend the deadline for selecting a thesis advisor by six months.</li><li>研究生最遲須於預計畢業當學期開學後二週內提出論文計畫書口試申請，開學後四週內舉行。若未通過者，必須於開學後八週內補提並通過。通過論文計畫書口試者，始得提畢業論文口試。確切日期每學期初由辦公室正式公告為主。口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。Graduate students must apply for their thesis proposal oral defense no later than two weeks after the start of the semester in which they plan to graduate, with the oral defense conducted within four weeks of the semester's start. If unsuccessful, they must reapply and pass within eight weeks of the semester's start. Only those who pass the thesis proposal oral defense may proceed to the final thesis oral defense. Specific dates are subject to official announcements at the beginning of each semester. The oral defense committee must include the thesis advisor (or co-advisors) and at least one additional member, either from within or outside the institution.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。Newly admitted graduate students must complete the academic research ethics education program as specified in the university's guidelines by the end of their first semester. The latest they can complete this program is before applying for the degree oral defense. Students who fail to complete the program cannot apply for the degree oral defense.</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。Matters not addressed herein shall be governed by the academic regulations of each major field of study.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

Students majoring in this field may substitute the MS core course "Econometrics" (3 credits) with "Financial Big Data Analysis and Forecasting." Required Courses: 3 credits, Compulsory Elective Courses: 12 credits, and Elective Courses: at least 6 credits.</li><li>跨學制課程3學分為限。A maximum of 3 credits can be earned from interdisciplinary courses.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

colspan="4"><ol><li>本碩士班畢業要求為最低總畢業學分數36學分，包含必修科目12學分、專業選修科目18學分、自由選修6學分；另加碩士論文一篇。申請上學期口試者須於12月底前完成論文口試，申請下學期口試者須於6月底前完成論文口試。Graduation requirements: Students must take a minimum of 36 credits, including 12 credits of GMS required courses, 18 credits of GMS elective courses, 6 credits of other MS and GMBA elective courses, and complete a master thesis. Oral defense of thesis must be completed by the end of December for first (Fall) semester graduation and by the end of June for second (Spring) semester graduation.</li><li>外籍碩士生須徵得授課老師同意，方可選修MS中文授課之選修課程。Foreign students who get approval from the instructor of the course may take elective courses in MS Chinese class.</li><li>碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者或官方語言為英語且經學程召集人同意，得申請免修。Students must take “English for Business Professionals” or “International Business Communication” arranged by the College (this course can't be used as credits for Graduation). If students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level, or students are from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand, have received bachelor degrees from listed countries, or official language is English and gets approval from the director of the discipline , these courses can be waived.</li><li>外籍碩士生需修畢本校國際語言文化中心開設之華語課程共兩學期、4學分（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生通過TOCFL Level 2以上，得申請免修。Foreign students are required to complete Mandarin Chinese courses 4 credits in two semester offered by International Language and Culture Center (ILCC).(The aforementioned is excluded from the graduation credits.) If the students pass TOCFL level 2 or above, may apply for a waiver.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first academic year and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>有關MS課程抵免換修相關事宜，依本碩士班相關規定辦理。Students should follow the regulations of MS program courses exemption and exchange.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以本院財務金融學群、會計學群、數位金融學群為限。Advisors need to be from discipline of Finance, Accounting, or Financial Technology.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研究生最遲須於預計畢業當學期開學後二週內提出論文計畫書口試申請，開學後四週內舉行。若未通過者，必須於開學後八週內補提並通過。通過論文計畫書口試者，始得提畢業論文口試。確切日期每學期初由辦公室正式公告為主。口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。Graduate students must submit their thesis proposal application no later than the first two weeks after the beginning of the semester in which they intend to graduate, and the proposal should be held within the first four weeks after the semester starts. In the event of a failure, students must resubmit and successfully pass their proposal by the eighth week of the semester. Only those who pass the thesis proposal are eligible to apply for the final thesis defense. The exact dates for each semester will be officially announced by the office at the beginning of the semester. The oral committee must consist of the advisor (including joint advisors) and one internal or external committee member.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam. </li></ol></td></tr></table>

**元智大學管理學院財務金融暨會計碩士班**

**（Master of Science in Finance and Accounting）**

**必修科目表**

**（113學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required and Elective Courses**

**(For students, entrance in academic year 113)**

113.06.05 一一二學年度第九次教務會議修訂通過

113.11.20 一一三學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subjects</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 First Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年Second Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>Required</p><p>Courses</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506 (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Semester Credit Subtotal</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）、「會計」（MS in Accounting）及「金融科技」（MS in Financial Technology）三個主修領域。The Master of Science Program in our institute includes three major fields of study: Finance (MS in Finance), Accounting (MS in Accounting), and Financial Technology (MS in Financial Technology).</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求各學程主修財務金融領域與會計領域最低總畢業學分數36學分，主修金融科技領域最低總畢業學分數24學分，以上三個主修領域皆須加碩士論文一篇。The graduation requirements for the MS Program specify a minimum of 36 credits for the Finance and Accounting fields, and 24 credits for the Financial Technology field. All three fields also require the completion of a master's thesis.</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目12學分、必選修科目15學分及選修科目至少6學分，主修會計領域必修科目12學分，必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少12學分，主修金融科技領域必修科目3學分，得以「金融大數據分析與預測」作為MS必修科目3學分，必選修科目12學分及選修科目至少6學分。Master’s students are required to complete 3 credits of MS core courses. The specific credit requirements for each field of study are as follows: Finance: 12 credits of required courses, 15 credits of required elective courses, and at least 6 credits of elective courses. Accounting: 12 credits of required courses, 9 credits of required elective courses, and at least 12 credits of elective courses. Financial Technology: 3 credits of required courses (the course Big Data Analysis and Forecasting in Finance can fulfill the MS core course requirement), 12 credits of required elective courses, and at least 6 credits of elective courses.</li><li>各學程相關規定：Specific Requirements:</li><li>主修財務金融：(i) 碩士生需在畢業前達到以下任何一項英語標準：(a) TOEIC 675分，或TOEFL iBT 68分，或CEFR 語言能力參考指標B2等級之英語檢定；(b) 修習本學程英語授課學分數達12學分且成績達70分(含)以上；(c) 國籍為美國、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭或英語為官方語言之國家，或曾於前述國家取(ii)碩士生經學群會議同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Finance: (i) Before graduation, students must meet one of the following English proficiency standards: (a) Achieve a TOEIC score of 675, TOEFL iBT score of 68, or CEFR B2 level in an English proficiency test. (b) Complete at least 12 credits of English-taught courses within the program with a minimum grade of 70. (c) Hold citizenship from or have studied in the U.S., U.K., Australia, New Zealand, or another country where English is an official language. (ii) With approval from the academic committee, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master’s programs offered by the institute. </li><li>主修會計學程：(i)「海外研習」與「企業實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。(ii) 碩士生經學程召集人同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Accounting: (i) Students may choose to recognize Overseas Study or Corporate Internship as a course, but only one of the two, and only once. (ii) With the approval of the program coordinator, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master's programs offered by the institute.</li></ol></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>主修金融科技學程：(i) 碩士生需修習過投資學或具備2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗，並提出修課證明或工作證明。若無修過投資學，亦無2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗者，需修習大學部「投資學」，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(ii) 碩士生需在學校單位或公私立培訓機構修習過程式設計課、程式培訓課程、或程式設計工作坊，並提出修課證明。若無修習過程式設計者，需修習大學部「Python程式設計」課程或類似課名課程，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(iii)碩士生經導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Financial Technology: (i) Students must have completed a course in Investments or possess at least two years of practical experience in finance-related work, providing proof of coursework or work experience. If neither requirement is met, students must take the undergraduate course Investments and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (ii) Students must have taken a programming course, training program, or workshop at the university or other training institutions and provide proof of completion. If no prior programming experience exists, students must take the undergraduate course Python Programming or a similar course and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (iii) With approval from their advisor or supervisor, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master’s programs offered by the institute.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Master's students must select their thesis advisor from professors in their major field of study.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Master's students are required to select their thesis advisor and complete the registration process by the end of the first academic year. They must also complete the thesis oral defense as stipulated.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。If a master's student fails two or more required courses by the end of the first academic year, they may extend the deadline for selecting a thesis advisor by six months.</li><li>研究生最遲須於預計畢業當學期開學後二週內提出論文計畫書口試申請，開學後四週內舉行。若未通過者，必須於開學後八週內補提並通過。通過論文計畫書口試者，始得提畢業論文口試。確切日期每學期初由辦公室正式公告為主。口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。Graduate students must apply for their thesis proposal oral defense no later than two weeks after the start of the semester in which they plan to graduate, with the oral defense conducted within four weeks of the semester's start. If unsuccessful, they must reapply and pass within eight weeks of the semester's start. Only those who pass the thesis proposal oral defense may proceed to the final thesis oral defense. Specific dates are subject to official announcements at the beginning of each semester. The oral defense committee must include the thesis advisor (or co-advisors) and at least one additional member, either from within or outside the institution.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。Newly admitted graduate students must complete the academic research ethics education program as specified in the university's guidelines by the end of their first semester. The latest they can complete this program is before applying for the degree oral defense. Students who fail to complete the program cannot apply for the degree oral defense.</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。Matters not addressed herein shall be governed by the academic regulations of each major field of study.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

Students majoring in this field may substitute the MS core course "Econometrics" (3 credits) with "Financial Big Data Analysis and Forecasting.”, Core courses: 3 credits, Mandatory elective courses: Choose 4 out of 5, totaling 12 credits, Elective courses: At least 6 credits</li><li>跨學制課程3學分為限。 A maximum of 3 credits from interdepartmental courses may be applied.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

including 12 credits of GMS required courses, 18 credits of GMS elective courses, 6 credits of other MS and GMBA elective courses, and complete a master thesis. Oral defense of thesis must be completed by the end of December for first (Fall) semester graduation and by the end of June for second (Spring) semester graduation.</li><li>外籍碩士生須徵得授課老師同意，方可選修MS中文授課之選修課程。Foreign students who get approval from the instructor of the course may take elective courses in MS Chinese class.</li><li>碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者或官方語言為英語且經學程召集人同意，得申請免修。Students must take “English for Business Professionals” or “International Business Communication” arranged by the College (this course can't be used as credits for Graduation). If students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level, or students are from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand, have received bachelor degrees from listed countries, or official language is English and gets approval from the director of the discipline , these courses can be waived.</li><li>外籍碩士生需修畢本校國際語言文化中心開設之華語課程共兩學期、4學分（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生通過TOCFL Level 2以上，得申請免修。Foreign students are required to complete Mandarin Chinese courses 4 credits in two semester offered by International Language and Culture Center (ILCC).(The aforementioned is excluded from the graduation credits.) If the students pass TOCFL level 2 or above, may apply for a waiver.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first academic year and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>有關MS課程抵免換修相關事宜，依本碩士班相關規定辦理。Students should follow the regulations of MS program courses exemption and exchange.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以本院財務金融學群、會計學群、數位金融學群為限。Advisors need to be from discipline of Finance, Accounting, or Financial Technology.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研究生最遲須於預計畢業當學期開學後二週內提出論文計畫書口試申請，開學後四週內舉行。若未通過者，必須於開學後八週內補提並通過。通過論文計畫書口試者，始得提畢業論文口試。確切日期每學期初由辦公室正式公告為主。口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。Graduate students must submit their thesis proposal application no later than the first two weeks after the beginning of the semester in which they intend to graduate, and the proposal should be held within the first four weeks after the semester starts. In the event of a failure, students must resubmit and successfully pass their proposal by the eighth week of the semester. Only those who pass the thesis proposal are eligible to apply for the final thesis defense. The exact dates for each semester will be officially announced by the office at the beginning of the semester. The oral committee must consist of the advisor (including joint advisors) and one internal or external committee member.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam. </li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

**元智大學管理學院財務金融暨會計碩士班**

**（Master of Science in Finance and Accounting）**

**必修科目表**

**（114學年度入學新生適用）**

**List of Required and Elective Courses**

**(For students, entrance in academic year 114)**

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subjects</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年 First Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年Second Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td></tr><tr><td><p>MS必修</p><p>科目 (3)</p></td><td><p>Required</p><p>Courses</p></td><td><p>計量經濟學</p><p>(Econometrics)</p><p>CM506 (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Semester Credit Subtotal</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>本院財務金融暨會計碩士班（MS Program）包括「財務金融」（MS in Finance）、「會計」（MS in Accounting）及「金融科技」（MS in Financial Technology）三個主修領域。The Master of Science Program in our institute includes three major fields of study: Finance (MS in Finance), Accounting (MS in Accounting), and Financial Technology (MS in Financial Technology).</li><li>本碩士班畢業要求各學程主修財務金融領域與會計領域最低總畢業學分數36學分，主修金融科技領域最低總畢業學分數24學分，以上三個主修領域皆須加碩士論文一篇。The graduation requirements for the MS Program specify a minimum of 36 credits for the Finance and Accounting fields, and 24 credits for the Financial Technology field. All three fields also require the completion of a master's thesis.</li><li>碩士生需完成MS必修科目3學分，主修財務金融領域必修科目12學分、必選修科目15學分及選修科目至少6學分，主修會計領域必修科目12學分，必選修科目9學分及選修科目至少12學分，主修金融科技領域必修科目3學分，得以「金融大數據分析與預測」作為MS必修科目3學分，必選修科目12學分及選修科目至少6學分。Master’s students are required to complete 3 credits of MS core courses. The specific credit requirements for each field of study are as follows: Finance: 12 credits of required courses, 15 credits of required elective courses, and at least 6 credits of elective courses. Accounting: 12 credits of required courses, 9 credits of required elective courses, and at least 12 credits of elective courses. Financial Technology: 3 credits of required courses (the course Big Data Analysis and Forecasting in Finance can fulfill the MS core course requirement), 12 credits of required elective courses, and at least 6 credits of elective courses.</li><li>各學程相關規定：Specific Requirements:</li><li>主修財務金融：(i) 碩士生需在畢業前達到以下任何一項英語標準：(a) TOEIC 675分，或TOEFL iBT 68分，或CEFR 語言能力參考指標B2等級之英語檢定；(b) 修習本學程英語授課學分數達12學分且成績達70分(含)以上；(c) 國籍為美國、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭或英語為官方語言之國家，或曾於前述國家取(ii)碩士生經學群會議同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Finance: (i) Before graduation, students must meet one of the following English proficiency standards: (a) Achieve a TOEIC score of 675, TOEFL iBT score of 68, or CEFR B2 level in an English proficiency test. (b) Complete at least 12 credits of English-taught courses within the program with a minimum grade of 70. (c) Hold citizenship from or have studied in the U.S., U.K., Australia, New Zealand, or another country where English is an official language. (ii) With approval from the academic committee, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master’s programs offered by the institute. </li><li>主修會計學程：(i)「海外研習」與「企業實習」僅能擇一認列一門課程，以一次為限。(ii) 碩士生經學程召集人同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Accounting: (i) Students may choose to recognize Overseas Study or Corporate Internship as a course, but only one of the two, and only once. (ii) With the approval of the program coordinator, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master's programs offered by the institute.</li><li>主修金融科技學程：(i) 碩士生需修習過投資學或具備2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗，並提出修課證明或工作證明。若無修過投資學，亦無2年以上(含2年)財金工作實務經驗者，需修習大學部「投資學」，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。</li><li>(ii) 碩士生需在學校單位或公私立培訓機構修習過程式設計課、程式培訓課程、或</li></ol></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>程式設計工作坊，並提出修課證明。若無修習過程式設計者，需修習大學部「Python</p><p>程式設計」課程或類似課名課程，並得及格成績(不列計畢業學分)。(iii)碩士生經</p><p>導師或指導教授同意，得選修本院各碩士班其它主修領域之課程。MS in Financial Technology: (i) Students must have completed a course in Investments or possess at least two years of practical experience in finance-related work, providing proof of coursework or work experience. If neither requirement is met, students must take the undergraduate course Investments and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (ii) Students must have taken a programming course, training program, or workshop at the university or other training institutions and provide proof of completion. If no prior programming experience exists, students must take the undergraduate course Python Programming or a similar course and achieve a passing grade (credits not counted toward graduation). (iii) With approval from their advisor or supervisor, students may enroll in courses from other fields of study within the master’s programs offered by the institute.</p><ol><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以其主修領域之老師為限。Master's students must select their thesis advisor from professors in their major field of study.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Master's students are required to select their thesis advisor and complete the registration process by the end of the first academic year. They must also complete the thesis oral defense as stipulated.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。If a master's student fails two or more required courses by the end of the first academic year, they may extend the deadline for selecting a thesis advisor by six months.</li><li>研究生最遲須於預計畢業當學期開學後二週內提出論文計畫書口試申請，開學後四週內舉行。若未通過者，必須於開學後八週內補提並通過。通過論文計畫書口試者，始得提畢業論文口試。確切日期每學期初由辦公室正式公告為主。口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。Graduate students must apply for their thesis proposal oral defense no later than two weeks after the start of the semester in which they plan to graduate, with the oral defense conducted within four weeks of the semester's start. If unsuccessful, they must reapply and pass within eight weeks of the semester's start. Only those who pass the thesis proposal oral defense may proceed to the final thesis oral defense. Specific dates are subject to official announcements at the beginning of each semester. The oral defense committee must include the thesis advisor (or co-advisors) and at least one additional member, either from within or outside the institution.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。Newly admitted graduate students must complete the academic research ethics education program as specified in the university's guidelines by the end of their first semester. The latest they can complete this program is before applying for the degree oral defense. Students who fail to complete the program cannot apply for the degree oral defense.</li><li>若有未盡事宜，悉依各主修領域之修業規定規範之。Matters not addressed herein shall be governed by the academic regulations of each major field of study.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

Students majoring in this field may substitute the MS core course "Econometrics" (3 credits) with "Financial Big Data Analysis and Forecasting.”, Core courses: 3 credits, Mandatory elective courses: Choose 4 out of 5, totaling 12 credits, Elective courses: At least 6 credits.</li><li>「主修本領域學生以本學程選修課程表所列示的課程作為優先選課目標，以滿足畢業學分要求。若於預訂畢業學期，本學程選修課程表的課程開課未能提供足夠畢業學分，得經學群會議通過，同意學生選修管理學院各碩士班學程所開的課程，至多得認列選修科目3學分」</li></ol><p>Students majoring in this field should prioritize enrolling in courses listed in the elective course schedule of this program to fulfill their graduation credit requirements. If, during the expected graduation semester, the elective courses offered by this program do not provide sufficient credits for graduation, students may, upon approval by the program committee, take courses offered by other master’s programs within the College of Management, with up to 3 credits recognized as elective courses.</p></td></tr></table>

including 12 credits of GMS required courses, 18 credits of GMS elective courses, 6 credits of other MS and GMBA elective courses, and complete a master thesis. Oral defense of thesis must be completed by the end of December for first (Fall) semester graduation and by the end of June for second (Spring) semester graduation.</li><li>外籍碩士生須徵得授課老師同意，方可選修MS中文授課之選修課程。Foreign students who get approval from the instructor of the course may take elective courses in MS Chinese class.</li><li>碩士生需修畢本院開設之「商用英文」或「跨國商業溝通」（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生TOEFL/ITP考試紙筆測驗520分以上(電腦測驗190分、新托福測驗IBT68以上)，或IELTS 6以上，或GMAT前70%以上，或GRE前70%以上，或多益(TOEIC)675分以上，或全民英檢中高級，得申請免修；此外，外籍學生若來自英語系國家（限美國、加拿大、英國、澳洲、紐西蘭）或曾於前述國家留學並取得大學以上學位者或官方語言為英語且經學程召集人同意，得申請免修。Students must take “English for Business Professionals” or “International Business Communication” arranged by the College (this course can't be used as credits for Graduation). If students reach TOEFL ITP/CBT/IBT 520/190/68, IELTS 6, GMAT 70% , GRE 70%, or TOEIC 675, GEPT High-Intermediate Level, or students are from the native English speaking countries of US, Canada, UK, Australia, and New Zealand, have received bachelor degrees from listed countries, or official language is English and gets approval from the director of the discipline , these courses can be waived.</li><li>外籍碩士生需修畢本校國際語言文化中心開設之華語課程共兩學期、4學分（不列計畢業學分）。惟，若該生通過TOCFL Level 2以上，得申請免修。Foreign students are required to complete Mandarin Chinese courses 4 credits in two semester offered by International Language and Culture Center (ILCC).(The aforementioned is excluded from the graduation credits.) If the students pass TOCFL level 2 or above, may apply for a waiver.</li><li>碩士生應於第一學年結束前選定論文指導教授及完成登錄程序，並依規定完成論文口試。Students must choose an advisor before the end of the first academic year and finish the required application process. Oral Examination of thesis needs to be completed according to regulations.</li><li>有關MS課程抵免換修相關事宜，依本碩士班相關規定辦理。Students should follow the regulations of MS program courses exemption and exchange.</li><li>碩士生選定之論文指導教授，應以本院財務金融學群、會計學群、數位金融學群為限。Advisors need to be from discipline of Finance, Accounting, or Financial Technology.</li><li>碩士生於第一學年結束前，有二科(含)以上必修課程未通過者，得延長半年選定論文指導教授。Graduated students who fail more than two required courses (including two courses) have to put off choosing the advisor of thesis writing for half year.</li><li>研究生最遲須於預計畢業當學期開學後二週內提出論文計畫書口試申請，開學後四週內舉行。若未通過者，必須於開學後八週內補提並通過。通過論文計畫書口試者，始得提畢業論文口試。確切日期每學期初由辦公室正式公告為主。口試委員須為指導教授（含共同指導教授）及一位校內或校外委員。Graduate students must submit their thesis proposal application no later than the first two weeks after the beginning of the semester in which they intend to graduate, and the proposal should be held within the first four weeks after the semester starts. In the event of a failure, students must resubmit and successfully pass their proposal by the eighth week of the semester. Only those who pass the thesis proposal are eligible to apply for the final thesis defense. The exact dates for each semester will be officially announced by the office at the beginning of the semester. The oral committee must consist of the advisor (including joint advisors) and one internal or external committee member.</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam. </li></ol></td></tr></table>
